function pk(e, t) {
    const n = Math.abs(t.top - e.y)
      , r = Math.abs(t.bottom - e.y)
      , s = Math.abs(t.right - e.x)
      , i = Math.abs(t.left - e.x);
    switch (Math.min(n, r, s, i)) {
    case i:
        return "left";
    case s:
        return "right";
    case n:
        return "top";
    case r:
        return "bottom";
    default:
        throw new Error("unreachable")
    }
}
function gk(e, t, n=5) {
    const r = [];
    switch (t) {
    case "top":
        r.push({
            x: e.x - n,
            y: e.y + n
        }, {
            x: e.x + n,
            y: e.y + n
        });
        break;
    case "bottom":
        r.push({
            x: e.x - n,
            y: e.y - n
        }, {
            x: e.x + n,
            y: e.y - n
        });
        break;
    case "left":
        r.push({
            x: e.x + n,
            y: e.y - n
        }, {
            x: e.x + n,
            y: e.y + n
        });
        break;
    case "right":
        r.push({
            x: e.x - n,
            y: e.y - n
        }, {
            x: e.x - n,
            y: e.y + n
        });
        break
    }
    return r
}

const Ro = e => {
    let t = 0;
    for (let n = 0; n < e.length; n++) {
        const r = e.charCodeAt(n);
        t = (t << 5) - t + r,
        t = t & t
    }
    return Math.abs(t)
}

    return n && E0(e, n) % 2 === 0 ? -r : r

      , n = parseInt(e.substr(2, 2), 16)
      , r = parseInt(e.substr(4, 2), 16);

}

}

var eM = {
    ArrowLeft: "prev",
    ArrowUp: "prev",
    ArrowRight: "next",
    ArrowDown: "next",
    PageUp: "first",
    Home: "first",
    PageDown: "last",
    End: "last"
};
function tM(e, t) {
    return t !== "rtl" ? e : e === "ArrowLeft" ? "ArrowRight" : e === "ArrowRight" ? "ArrowLeft" : e
}
function nM(e, t, n) {
    const r = tM(e.key, n);
    if (!(t === "vertical" && ["ArrowLeft", "ArrowRight"].includes(r)) && !(t === "horizontal" && ["ArrowUp", "ArrowDown"].includes(r)))
        return eM[r]
}
function Kw(e, t=!1) {
    const n = document.activeElement;
    for (const r of e)
        if (r === n || (r.focus({
            preventScroll: t
        }),
        document.activeElement !== n))
            return
}
function rM(e, t) {
    return e.map( (n, r) => e[(t + r) % e.length])
}

function w_(e) {

    if (!e)
        return "C";

      , n = (((s = t[0]) == null ? void 0 : s[0]) || "").toUpperCase()
      , r = (((i = t[1]) == null ? void 0 : i[0]) || (t.length > 1 ? t.at(-1)[0] : "")).toUpperCase();
    return (n + r).trim() || "C"
}
function j_(e) {
    const t = e || "Customer";
    let n = 0;
    for (let r = 0; r < t.length; r++)
        n = (n * 31 + t.charCodeAt(r)) % 360;
    return n
}

    const n = t.additionalDigits == null ? hD : Number(t.additionalDigits);
    if (n !== 2 && n !== 1 && n !== 0)
        throw new RangeError("additionalDigits must be 0, 1 or 2");
    if (e instanceof Date || typeof e == "object" && Object.prototype.toString.call(e) === "[object Date]")
        return new Date(e.getTime());
    if (typeof e == "number" || Object.prototype.toString.call(e) === "[object Number]")
        return new Date(e);
    if (Object.prototype.toString.call(e) !== "[object String]")
        return new Date(NaN);
    const r = pD(e)
      , {year: s, restDateString: i} = gD(r.date, n)
      , a = xD(i, s);
    if (a === null || isNaN(a.getTime()))
        return new Date(NaN);
    if (a) {
        const l = a.getTime();
        let c = 0, d;
        if (r.time && (c = vD(r.time),
        c === null || isNaN(c)))
            return new Date(NaN);
        if (r.timeZone || t.timeZone) {
            if (d = ej(r.timeZone || t.timeZone, new Date(l + c)),
            isNaN(d))
                return new Date(NaN)
        } else
            d = sg(new Date(l + c)),
            d = sg(new Date(l + c + d));
        return new Date(l + c + d)
    } else
        return new Date(NaN)
}
function pD(e) {
    const t = {};
    let n = ht.dateTimePattern.exec(e), r;
    if (n ? (t.date = n[1],
    r = n[3]) : (n = ht.datePattern.exec(e),
    n ? (t.date = n[1],
    r = n[2]) : (t.date = null,
    r = e)),
    r) {
        const s = ht.timeZone.exec(r);
        s ? (t.time = r.replace(s[1], ""),
        t.timeZone = s[1].trim()) : t.time = r
    }
    return t
}
function gD(e, t) {
    if (e) {
        const n = ht.YYY[t]
          , r = ht.YYYYY[t];
        let s = ht.YYYY.exec(e) || r.exec(e);
        if (s) {
            const i = s[1];
            return {
                year: parseInt(i, 10),
                restDateString: e.slice(i.length)
            }
        }
        if (s = ht.YY.exec(e) || n.exec(e),
        s) {
            const i = s[1];
            return {
                year: parseInt(i, 10) * 100,
                restDateString: e.slice(i.length)
            }
        }
    }
    return {
        year: null
    }
}
function xD(e, t) {
    if (t === null)
        return null;
    let n, r, s;
    if (!e || !e.length)
        return n = new Date(0),
        n.setUTCFullYear(t),
        n;
    let i = ht.MM.exec(e);
    if (i)
        return n = new Date(0),
        r = parseInt(i[1], 10) - 1,
        ag(t, r) ? (n.setUTCFullYear(t, r),
        n) : new Date(NaN);
    if (i = ht.DDD.exec(e),
    i) {
        n = new Date(0);
        const a = parseInt(i[1], 10);
        return jD(t, a) ? (n.setUTCFullYear(t, 0, a),
        n) : new Date(NaN)
    }
    if (i = ht.MMDD.exec(e),
    i) {
        n = new Date(0),
        r = parseInt(i[1], 10) - 1;
        const a = parseInt(i[2], 10);
        return ag(t, r, a) ? (n.setUTCFullYear(t, r, a),
        n) : new Date(NaN)
    }
    if (i = ht.Www.exec(e),
    i)
        return s = parseInt(i[1], 10) - 1,
        lg(s) ? ig(t, s) : new Date(NaN);
    if (i = ht.WwwD.exec(e),
    i) {
        s = parseInt(i[1], 10) - 1;
        const a = parseInt(i[2], 10) - 1;
        return lg(s, a) ? ig(t, s, a) : new Date(NaN)
    }
    return null
}
function vD(e) {
    let t, n, r = ht.HH.exec(e);
    if (r)
        return t = parseFloat(r[1].replace(",", ".")),
        yu(t) ? t % 24 * vu : NaN;
    if (r = ht.HHMM.exec(e),
    r)
        return t = parseInt(r[1], 10),
        n = parseFloat(r[2].replace(",", ".")),
        yu(t, n) ? t % 24 * vu + n * og : NaN;
    if (r = ht.HHMMSS.exec(e),
    r) {
        t = parseInt(r[1], 10),
        n = parseInt(r[2], 10);
        const s = parseFloat(r[3].replace(",", "."));
        return yu(t, n, s) ? t % 24 * vu + n * og + s * 1e3 : NaN
    }
    return null
}
function ig(e, t, n) {
    t = t || 0,
    n = n || 0;
    const r = new Date(0);
    r.setUTCFullYear(e, 0, 4);
    const s = r.getUTCDay() || 7
      , i = t * 7 + n + 1 - s;
    return r.setUTCDate(r.getUTCDate() + i),
    r
}
const yD = [31, 28, 31, 30, 31, 30, 31, 31, 30, 31, 30, 31]
  , wD = [31, 29, 31, 30, 31, 30, 31, 31, 30, 31, 30, 31];
function tj(e) {
    return e % 400 === 0 || e % 4 === 0 && e % 100 !== 0
}
function ag(e, t, n) {
    if (t < 0 || t > 11)
        return !1;
    if (n != null) {
        if (n < 1)
            return !1;
        const r = tj(e);
        if (r && n > wD[t] || !r && n > yD[t])
            return !1
    }
    return !0
}
function jD(e, t) {
    if (t < 1)
        return !1;
    const n = tj(e);
    return !(n && t > 366 || !n && t > 365)
}
function lg(e, t) {
    return !(e < 0 || e > 52 || t != null && (t < 0 || t > 6))
}
function yu(e, t, n) {
    return !(e < 0 || e >= 25 || t != null && (t < 0 || t >= 60) || n != null && (n < 0 || n >= 60))
}
function Rl(e, t, n) {
    e = mD(e, n);
    const r = ej(t, e, !0)
      , s = new Date(e.getTime() - r)
      , i = new Date(0);
    return i.setFullYear(s.getUTCFullYear(), s.getUTCMonth(), s.getUTCDate()),
    i.setHours(s.getUTCHours(), s.getUTCMinutes(), s.getUTCSeconds(), s.getUTCMilliseconds()),
    i
}

}

                            className: [n === "week" ? "h-64" : "h-36", "p-2 border -m-[0.5px] text-left overflow-hidden", "hover:bg-gray-50 transition", B ? "bg-gray-50/40 text-gray-400" : "bg-white", R ? "ring-2 ring-primary/60 z-[1]" : ""].join(" "),
                            "data-testid": `day-cell-${L}`,
                            children: [o.jsxs("div", {
                                className: "flex items-center justify-between mb-1",
                                children: [o.jsx("button", {
                                    className: "text-xs font-medium",
                                    onClick: () => C(P),
                                    "data-testid": `day-number-${L}`,
                                    children: We(P, "d")
                                }), !!F.length && o.jsx(jo, {
                                    className: "text-[10px] py-0 px-1.5",
                                    "data-testid": `day-badge-${L}`,
                                    children: F.length
                                })]
                            }), o.jsxs("div", {
                                className: "space-y-1",
                                children: [F.slice(0, n === "week" ? 8 : 3).map(_ => o.jsxs("div", {
                                    draggable: !0,
                                    onDragStart: $ => O($, _),
                                    className: ["text-[11px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded line-clamp-1 cursor-move", SD(_.status)].join(" "),
                                    onClick: $ => {
                                        $.stopPropagation(),
                                        e(`/jobs/${_.id}`)
                                    }
                                    ,
                                    title: `${_.title}${_.customer_name ? " — " + _.customer_name : ""}`,
                                    "data-testid": `job-pill-${_.id}`,
                                    children: [_.title, _.customer_name ? ` — ${_.customer_name}` : ""]
                                }, _.id)), F.length > (n === "week" ? 8 : 3) && o.jsxs("button", {
                                    className: "text-[10px] text-gray-500",
                                    onClick: () => C(P),
                                    "data-testid": `more-jobs-${L}`,
                                    children: ["+", F.length - (n === "week" ? 8 : 3), " more…"]
                                })]
                            })]
                        }, L)
                    }
                    )
                })]
            })
        }), o.jsx(Lr, {
            open: !!b,
            onOpenChange: P => C(P ? b : null),
            children: o.jsxs(Gn, {
                className: "max-w-lg",
                children: [o.jsx(Jn, {
                    children: o.jsx(Xn, {
                        "data-testid": "day-modal-title",
                        children: b ? We(b, "EEEE, d MMM yyyy") : "Day"
                    })
                }), M.length === 0 ? o.jsx("div", {
                    className: "text-sm text-gray-500",
                    "data-testid": "no-jobs-message",
                    children: "No jobs scheduled."
                }) : o.jsx("div", {
                    className: "space-y-2",
                    children: M.map(P => o.jsx(je, {
                        href: `/jobs/${P.id}`,
                        children: o.jsxs("a", {
                            className: "block border rounded p-2 hover:bg-gray-50",
                            "data-testid": `day-job-${P.id}`,
                            children: [o.jsx("div", {
                                className: "text-sm font-medium",
                                children: P.title
                            }), o.jsxs("div", {
                                className: "text-xs text-gray-600",
                                children: [P.customer_name || "—", " • ", ( () => {
                                    try {
                                        console.log(`[Desktop Modal] Job ${P.title}: raw=${P.scheduled_at}`);
                                        const L = P.scheduled_at.includes("T") ? P.scheduled_at : P.scheduled_at.replace(" ", "T").replace("+00", "Z")
                                          , F = Gs(L)
                                          , B = Rl(F, "Australia/Melbourne")
                                          , R = We(B, "h:mm a");
                                        return console.log(`[Desktop Modal] Job ${P.title}: local=${R}`),
                                        R
                                    } catch (L) {
                                        return console.error(`[Desktop Modal] Time parse error for ${P.title}:`, L),
                                        new Date(P.scheduled_at).toLocaleTimeString([], {
                                            hour: "2-digit",
                                            minute: "2-digit"
                                        })
                                    }
                                }
                                )()]
                            })]
                        })
                    }, P.id))
                })]
            })
        })]
    })
}

function nj({items: e, onAdd: t, onUpdate: n, onDelete: r}) {
    const [s,i] = u.useState({
        description: "",
        quantity: 1,
        unit_price: 0
    })
      , a = u.useMemo( () => e.reduce( (l, c) => l + Number(c.quantity) * Number(c.unit_price), 0), [e]);
    return o.jsxs("div", {
        className: "space-y-3",
        children: [o.jsx("div", {
            className: "table-wrap",
            children: o.jsxs("table", {
                className: "w-full text-sm",
                children: [o.jsx("thead", {
                    className: "bg-gray-50",
                    children: o.jsxs("tr", {
                        children: [o.jsx("th", {
                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-left",
                            children: "Description"
                        }), o.jsx("th", {
                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-right",
                            children: "Qty"
                        }), o.jsx("th", {
                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-right",
                            children: "Unit"
                        }), o.jsx("th", {
                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-right",
                            children: "Line"
                        }), o.jsx("th", {
                            className: "px-3 py-2"
                        })]
                    })
                }), o.jsx("tbody", {
                    className: "divide-y",
                    children: e.map(l => o.jsxs("tr", {
                        children: [o.jsx("td", {
                            className: "px-3 py-2",
                            children: l.description
                        }), o.jsx("td", {
                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-right",
                            children: Number(l.quantity).toFixed(2)
                        }), o.jsxs("td", {
                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-right",
                            children: ["$", Number(l.unit_price).toFixed(2)]
                        }), o.jsxs("td", {
                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-right",
                            children: ["$", (Number(l.quantity) * Number(l.unit_price)).toFixed(2)]
                        }), o.jsx("td", {
                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-right",
                            children: o.jsx(z, {
                                variant: "ghost",
                                onClick: () => r(l.id),
                                children: "Delete"
                            })
                        })]
                    }, l.id))
                })]
            })
        }), o.jsxs("div", {
            className: "form-grid",
            children: [o.jsx("div", {
                className: "col-span-2",
                children: o.jsx(V, {
                    placeholder: "Description",
                    value: s.description,
                    onChange: l => i({
                        ...s,
                        description: l.target.value
                    })
                })
            }), o.jsx(V, {
                type: "number",
                step: "0.01",
                placeholder: "Qty",
                value: s.quantity,
                onChange: l => i({
                    ...s,
                    quantity: Number(l.target.value)
                })
            }), o.jsx(V, {
                type: "number",
                step: "0.01",
                placeholder: "Unit Price",
                value: s.unit_price,
                onChange: l => i({
                    ...s,
                    unit_price: Number(l.target.value)
                })
            }), o.jsx(z, {
                onClick: async () => {
                    s.description && (await t(s),
                    i({
                        description: "",
                        quantity: 1,
                        unit_price: 0
                    }))
                }
                ,
                children: "Add item"
            })]
        }), o.jsx("div", {
            className: "text-right text-sm",
            children: o.jsxs("div", {
                className: "font-medium",
                children: ["Subtotal: $", a.toFixed(2)]
            })
        })]
    })
}
function cg() {
    de("/quotes/new");
    const [e,t] = de("/quotes/:id/edit")
      , [,n] = qe()
      , r = t == null ? void 0 : t.id
      , [s,i] = u.useState("")
      , [a,l] = u.useState("")
      , [c,d] = u.useState("")
      , [f,m] = u.useState("draft")
      , [h,w] = u.useState([])
      , [j,p] = u.useState([])
      , [v,x] = u.useState(!0)
      , [g,y] = u.useState(!1)
      , [N,S] = u.useState(null);
    u.useEffect( () => {
        (async () => {
            try {
                const b = await Bn.getAll();
                if (p(b || []),
                r) {
                    const C = await jt.get(r);
                    i(C.title || ""),
                    l(C.customer_id || ""),
                    d(C.notes || ""),
                    m(C.status || "draft"),
                    w(C.items || [])
                }
            } catch (b) {
                S(b.message)
            } finally {
                x(!1)
            }
        }
        )()
    }
    , [r]);
    async function k() {
        y(!0),
        S(null);
        try {
            if (r)
                await jt.update(r, {
                    title: s,
                    customerId: a,
                    notes: c,
                    status: f
                }),
                n(`/quotes/${r}`);
            else {
                const b = await jt.create({
                    title: s,
                    customerId: a,
                    notes: c
                });
                n(`/quotes/${b.id}/edit`)
            }
        } catch (b) {
            S(b.message || "Failed")
        } finally {
            y(!1)
        }
    }
    return v ? o.jsx("div", {
        className: "page",
        children: "Loading…"
    }) : o.jsxs("div", {
        className: "page space-y-6",
        children: [o.jsxs("div", {
            className: "header-row",
            children: [o.jsx("h1", {
                className: "text-2xl font-bold",
                children: r ? "Edit Quote" : "New Quote"
            }), o.jsx("div", {
                className: "header-actions",
                children: o.jsx(z, {
                    onClick: k,
                    disabled: g,
                    "data-mobile-full": "true",
                    children: g ? "Saving…" : "Save"
                })
            })]
        }), N && o.jsx("div", {
            className: "text-red-600",
            children: N
        }), o.jsxs(X, {
            children: [o.jsx(fe, {
                children: o.jsx(he, {
                    children: "Details"
                })
            }), o.jsxs(Z, {
                className: "form-grid",
                children: [o.jsx("div", {
                    className: "col-span-2",
                    children: o.jsx(V, {
                        placeholder: "Title",
                        value: s,
                        onChange: b => i(b.target.value)
                    })
                }), o.jsxs("div", {
                    children: [o.jsx("label", {
                        className: "block text-sm font-medium mb-1",
                        children: "Customer"
                    }), o.jsxs("select", {
                        className: "w-full border rounded p-2",
                        value: a,
                        onChange: b => l(b.target.value),
                        children: [o.jsx("option", {
                            value: "",
                            children: "Select customer…"
                        }), j.map(b => o.jsx("option", {
                            value: b.id,
                            children: b.name
                        }, b.id))]
                    })]
                }), o.jsxs("div", {
                    className: "col-span-2",
                    children: [o.jsx("label", {
                        className: "block text-sm font-medium mb-1",
                        children: "Notes"
                    }), o.jsx(qn, {
                        rows: 3,
                        value: c,
                        onChange: b => d(b.target.value)
                    })]
                }), o.jsxs("div", {
                    children: [o.jsx("label", {
                        className: "block text-sm font-medium mb-1",
                        children: "Status"
                    }), o.jsxs("select", {
                        className: "w-full border rounded p-2",
                        value: f,
                        onChange: b => m(b.target.value),
                        children: [o.jsx("option", {
                            value: "draft",
                            children: "draft"
                        }), o.jsx("option", {
                            value: "sent",
                            children: "sent"
                        }), o.jsx("option", {
                            value: "accepted",
                            children: "accepted"
                        }), o.jsx("option", {
                            value: "rejected",
                            children: "rejected"
                        })]
                    })]
                })]
            })]
        }), r && o.jsxs(X, {
            children: [o.jsx(fe, {
                children: o.jsx(he, {
                    children: "Line Items"
                })
            }), o.jsx(Z, {
                className: "card-pad",
                children: o.jsx(nj, {
                    items: h,
                    onAdd: async b => {
                        await jt.addItem(r, b);
                        const C = await jt.get(r);
                        w(C.items || [])
                    }
                    ,
                    onUpdate: async (b, C) => {
                        await jt.updateItem(r, b, C);
                        const M = await jt.get(r);
                        w(M.items || [])
                    }
                    ,
                    onDelete: async b => {
                        await jt.deleteItem(r, b);
                        const C = await jt.get(r);
                        w(C.items || [])
                    }
                })
            })]
        })]
    })
}
function PD() {
    const [e,t] = de("/quotes/:id")
      , [,n] = qe()
      , r = t == null ? void 0 : t.id
      , [s,i] = u.useState(null)
      , [a,l] = u.useState(!0)
      , [c,d] = u.useState(null);
    u.useEffect( () => {
        r && (async () => {
            try {
                const h = await jt.get(r);
                i(h)
            } catch (h) {
                d(h.message)
            } finally {
                l(!1)
            }
        }
        )()
    }
    , [r]);
    async function f() {
        if (r)
            try {
                await jt.accept(r);
                const h = await jt.get(r);
                i(h)
            } catch (h) {
                d(h.message)
            }
    }
    async function m() {
        if (r)
            try {
                const h = await jt.convertToJob(r);
                n(`/jobs/${h.jobId}`)
            } catch (h) {
                d(h.message)
            }
    }
    return a ? o.jsx("div", {
        className: "page",
        children: "Loading…"
    }) : s ? o.jsxs("div", {
        className: "page space-y-6",
        children: [o.jsxs("div", {
            className: "header-row",
            children: [o.jsx("h1", {
                className: "text-2xl font-bold",
                children: s.title
            }), o.jsxs("div", {
                className: "header-actions",
                children: [o.jsx(je, {
                    href: `/quotes/${r}/edit`,

                        children: o.jsx(z, {
                            variant: "outline",
                            children: "Edit"
                        })
                    })
                }), s.status === "sent" && o.jsx(z, {
                    onClick: f,
                    children: "Accept"
                }), s.status === "accepted" && o.jsx(z, {
                    onClick: m,
                    children: "Convert to Job"
                })]
            })]
        }), c && o.jsx("div", {
            className: "text-red-600",
            children: c
        }), o.jsxs("div", {
            className: "grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6",
            children: [o.jsxs("div", {
                className: "lg:col-span-2 space-y-6",
                children: [o.jsxs(X, {
                    children: [o.jsx(fe, {
                        children: o.jsx(he, {
                            children: "Details"
                        })
                    }), o.jsxs(Z, {
                        className: "card-pad space-y-4",
                        children: [o.jsxs("div", {
                            children: [o.jsx("strong", {
                                children: "Customer:"
                            }), " ", s.customer_name]
                        }), o.jsxs("div", {
                            children: [o.jsx("strong", {
                                children: "Status:"
                            }), " ", o.jsx("span", {
                                className: "capitalize",
                                children: s.status
                            })]
                        }), s.notes && o.jsxs("div", {
                            children: [o.jsx("strong", {
                                children: "Notes:"
                            }), " ", s.notes]
                        })]
                    })]
                }), o.jsxs(X, {
                    children: [o.jsx(fe, {
                        children: o.jsx(he, {
                            children: "Line Items"
                        })
                    }), o.jsx(Z, {
                        className: "card-pad",
                        children: o.jsx("div", {
                            className: "table-wrap",
                            children: o.jsxs("table", {
                                className: "w-full text-sm",
                                children: [o.jsx("thead", {
                                    className: "bg-gray-50",
                                    children: o.jsxs("tr", {
                                        children: [o.jsx("th", {
                                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-left",
                                            children: "Description"
                                        }), o.jsx("th", {
                                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-right",
                                            children: "Qty"
                                        }), o.jsx("th", {
                                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-right",
                                            children: "Unit"
                                        }), o.jsx("th", {
                                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-right",
                                            children: "Total"
                                        })]
                                    })
                                }), o.jsxs("tbody", {
                                    className: "divide-y",
                                    children: [(s.items || []).map(h => o.jsxs("tr", {
                                        children: [o.jsx("td", {
                                            className: "px-3 py-2",
                                            children: h.description
                                        }), o.jsx("td", {
                                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-right",
                                            children: Number(h.quantity).toFixed(2)
                                        }), o.jsxs("td", {
                                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-right",
                                            children: ["$", Number(h.unit_price).toFixed(2)]
                                        }), o.jsxs("td", {
                                            className: "px-3 py-2 text-right",
                                            children: ["$", (Number(h.quantity) * Number(h.unit_price)).toFixed(2)]
                                        })]
                                    }, h.id)), (!s.items || s.items.length === 0) && o.jsx("tr", {
                                        children: o.jsx("td", {
                                            colSpan: 4,
                                            className: "px-3 py-8 text-center text-gray-500",
                                            children: "No items"
                                        })
                                    })]
                                })]
                            })
                        })
                    })]
                })]
            }), o.jsx("div", {
                className: "space-y-6",
                children: o.jsxs(X, {
                    children: [o.jsx(fe, {
                        children: o.jsx(he, {
                            children: "Summary"
                        })
                    }), o.jsx(Z, {

                            className: "space-y-2 text-sm",

                                })]
                            }), o.jsxs("div", {
                                className: "flex justify-between font-medium text-lg",
                                children: [o.jsx("span", {
                                    children: "Total:"
                                }), o.jsxs("span", {
                                    children: ["$", Number(s.total || 0).toFixed(2)]
                                })]
                            })]
                        })
                    })]
                })
            })]
        })]
    }) : o.jsx("div", {
        className: "page",
        children: "Quote not found"
    })

function FD() {
    var S, k;
    const [e,t] = de("/jobs/:id")
      , [,n] = qe()
      , r = Ke()
      , s = t == null ? void 0 : t.id
      , [i,a] = u.useState(null)
      , [l,c] = u.useState([])
      , [d,f] = u.useState(null)
      , [m,h] = u.useState(!0)
      , [w,j] = u.useState(!1)
      , [p,v] = u.useState(!1)
      , [x,g] = u.useState(null);
    if (u.useEffect( () => {
        (async () => {
            try {
                const [b,C] = await Promise.all([Q(`/api/jobs/${s}`), rs.list(s)]);
                a(b),
                c(C)
            } catch (b) {
                f((b == null ? void 0 : b.message) || "Failed to load job")
            } finally {
                h(!1)
            }
        }
        )()
    }
    , [s]),
    m)
        return o.jsx("div", {
            className: "p-6",
            children: "Loading…"
        });
    if (d)
        return o.jsx("div", {
            className: "p-6 text-red-600",
            children: d
        });
    if (!i)
        return null;
    const y = (i.status || "new").replace("_", " ");
    function N(b, C, M, O) {
        if (!C && !b && !M && !O) {
            console.warn("No navigation destination available");
            return
        }
        const D = /iPad|iPhone|iPod/.test(navigator.userAgent) && !window.MSStream
          , T = typeof M == "number";
        try {
            if (D) {
                const L = T ? `maps://?q=${encodeURIComponent(b)}&daddr=${M},${O}` : `maps://?q=${encodeURIComponent(C || b)}`;
                window.location.href = L;
                return
            }
            const U = T ? `${M},${O}` : C || b
              , P = `https://www.google.com/maps/dir/?api=1&destination=${encodeURIComponent(U)}`;

    var p, v;

    })

        name: "",
        role: "",
        phone: "",
        avatar_url: ""
    })

        name: "",

        street: "",
        suburb: "",
        state: "",

    })

        current: "",
        next: "",

    })

        if (!n)
            return;
        const x = n.user || {}
          , g = n.org || {};
        i({
            name: x.name || "",

        }),

                name: s.name || null,
                role: s.role || null,
                phone: s.phone || null,

            }),

                description: (x == null ? void 0 : x.message) || "Failed to update profile",
                variant: "destructive"
            })
        } finally {
            m(!1)
        }
    }
    async function w() {

            t({
                title: "Error",
                description: "Passwords do not match",
                variant: "destructive"
            });

        }

            }),

            }),

                description: "Your password has been updated successfully."
            })

                description: (x == null ? void 0 : x.message) || "Failed to change password",

            })

    }

    async function j() {
        w(!0);

            const p = await Cl.create({
                email: s,

            });
            i(""),
            l(""),
